insert into submit_work (work_id,user_account,work_content,work_filepath) values ('2','1640664100','import java.awt.Color;
import java.awt.Font;
import java.awt.event.ActionEvent;
import java.awt.event.ActionListener;
import java.util.Random;

import javax.swing.JFrame;
import javax.swing.JMenu;
import javax.swing.JMenuBar;
import javax.swing.JMenuItem;
import javax.swing.JScrollPane;
import javax.swing.JTextArea;
import javax.swing.JTextField;
import javax.swing.KeyStroke;


public class Demo4 extends JFrame{
	private JScrollPane scroll_bar;
	private JTextField edit_text_area;
	private int s;
	public Demo4() {
		initMenuBar();
		initEdit();
		this.setSize(300,200);
		this.setTitle(\"自定义文本编辑器\");
		this.add(scroll_bar);
		this.setVisible(true);
		this.setLocationRelativeTo(null);
		this.setDefaultCloseOperation(JFrame.EXIT_ON_CLOSE);
	}
	private void initEdit() {
	    edit_text_area = new JTextField();
	    edit_text_area.setFont(new Font(\"楷体\",Font.PLAIN,16));
		scroll_bar = new JScrollPane(edit_text_area);
		scroll_bar.setVerticalScrollBarPolicy(JScrollPane.VERTICAL_SCROLLBAR_AS_NEEDED);
	}
	public void initMenuBar() {
		JMenuBar menuBar=new JMenuBar();
		setJMenuBar(menuBar);
		JMenu menu_File=new JMenu(\"菜单\");
		menuBar.add(menu_File);
		JMenuItem item_exit=new JMenuItem(\"退出\");
		JMenuItem item_changecolor=new JMenuItem(\"改变颜色\");
		JMenuItem item_changefont=new JMenuItem(\"改变字体\");
		JMenuItem item_changeBig=new JMenuItem(\"改变大小\");
		menu_File.add(item_changecolor);
		menu_File.add(item_changefont);
		menu_File.add(item_changeBig);
		menu_File.add(item_exit);
		item_changefont.addActionListener(new ActionListener(){
			public void actionPerformed(ActionEvent e) {
				if(s!=0){
				edit_text_area.setFont(new Font(\"宋体\",Font.PLAIN,s));
				}else{
				edit_text_area.setFont(new Font(\"宋体\",Font.PLAIN,16));
				}
			}	
		});
		item_changecolor.addActionListener(new ActionListener(){
			public void actionPerformed(ActionEvent e) {
				int sum=(int) (Math.random()*250);
				edit_text_area.setForeground(new Color(255-sum,255-sum,255-sum));
			}	
		});
		item_changeBig.addActionListener(new ActionListener(){
			public void actionPerformed(ActionEvent e) {
				Random random=new Random();
				s=(int) (Math.random()*20+1);
				System.out.println(s);
				edit_text_area.setFont(new Font(\"宋体\",Font.PLAIN,s));
			}	
		});
		item_exit.addActionListener(new ActionListener(){
			public void actionPerformed(ActionEvent e) {
				System.exit(0);
			}	
		});
	}

insert into submit_work (work_id,user_account,work_content,work_filepath) values ('2','1640664100','import java.awt.Color;
import java.awt.Font;
import java.awt.event.ActionEvent;
import java.awt.event.ActionListener;
import java.util.Random;

import javax.swing.JFrame;
import javax.swing.JMenu;
import javax.swing.JMenuBar;
import javax.swing.JMenuItem;
import javax.swing.JScrollPane;
import javax.swing.JTextArea;
import javax.swing.JTextField;
import javax.swing.KeyStroke;


public class Demo4 extends JFrame{
	private JScrollPane scroll_bar;
	private JTextField edit_text_area;
	private int s;
	public Demo4() {
		initMenuBar();
		initEdit();
		this.setSize(300,200);
		this.setTitle(\"自定义文本编辑器\");
		this.add(scroll_bar);
		this.setVisible(true);
		this.setLocationRelativeTo(null);
		this.setDefaultCloseOperation(JFrame.EXIT_ON_CLOSE);
	}
	private void initEdit() {
	    edit_text_area = new JTextField();
	    edit_text_area.setFont(new Font(\"楷体\",Font.PLAIN,16));
		scroll_bar = new JScrollPane(edit_text_area);
		scroll_bar.setVerticalScrollBarPolicy(JScrollPane.VERTICAL_SCROLLBAR_AS_NEEDED);
	}
	public void initMenuBar() {
		JMenuBar menuBar=new JMenuBar();
		setJMenuBar(menuBar);
		JMenu menu_File=new JMenu(\"菜单\");
		menuBar.add(menu_File);
		JMenuItem item_exit=new JMenuItem(\"退出\");
		JMenuItem item_changecolor=new JMenuItem(\"改变颜色\");

	private JTextField edit_text_area;

		initEdit();

		this.add(scroll_bar);

		this.setLocationRelativeTo(null);
		this.setDefaultCloseOperation(JFrame.EXIT_ON_CLOSE);
	}

insert into submit_work (work_id,user_account,work_content) values ('2','1640664100','import java.awt.Color;
import java.awt.Font;
import java.awt.event.ActionEvent;
import java.awt.event.ActionListener;
import java.util.Random;

import javax.swing.JFrame;
import javax.swing.JMenu;
import javax.swing.JMenuBar;
import javax.swing.JMenuItem;
import javax.swing.JScrollPane;
import javax.swing.JTextArea;
import javax.swing.JTextField;
import javax.swing.KeyStroke;


public class Demo4 extends JFrame{
	private JScrollPane scroll_bar;
	private JTextField edit_text_area;
	private int s;
	public Demo4() {
		initMenuBar();
		initEdit();
		this.setSize(300,200);
		this.setTitle(\"自定义文本编辑器\");
		this.add(scroll_bar);
		this.setVisible(true);
		this.setLocationRelativeTo(null);
		this.setDefaultCloseOperation(JFrame.EXIT_ON_CLOSE);
	}
	private void initEdit() {
	    edit_text_area = new JTextField();
	    edit_text_area.setFont(new Font(\"楷体\",Font.PLAIN,16));
		scroll_bar = new JScrollPane(edit_text_area);
		scroll_bar.setVerticalScrollBarPolicy(JScrollPane.VERTICAL_SCROLLBAR_AS_NEEDED);
	}
	public void initMenuBar() {
		JMenuBar menuBar=new JMenuBar();
		setJMenuBar(menuBar);
		JMenu menu_File=new JMenu(\"菜单\");
		menuBar.add(menu_File);
		JMenuItem item_exit=new JMenuItem(\"退出\");
		JMenuItem item_changecolor=new JMenuItem(\"改变颜色\");
		JMenuItem item_changefont=new JMenuItem(\"改变字体\");
		JMenuItem item_changeBig=new JMenuItem(\"改变大小\");
		menu_File.add(item_changecolor);
		menu_File.add(item_changefont);
		menu_File.add(item_changeBig);
		menu_File.add(item_exit);
		item_changefont.addActionListener(new ActionListener(){
			public void actionPerformed(ActionEvent e) {
				if(s!=0){
				edit_text_area.setFont(new Font(\"宋体\",Font.PLAIN,s));
				}else{
				edit_text_area.setFont(new Font(\"宋体\",Font.PLAIN,16));
				}
			}	
		});
		item_changecolor.addActionListener(new ActionListener(){
			public void actionPerformed(ActionEvent e) {
				int sum=(int) (Math.random()*250);
				edit_text_area.setForeground(new Color(255-sum,255-sum,255-sum));
			}	
		});
		item_changeBig.addActionListener(new ActionListener(){
			public void actionPerformed(ActionEvent e) {
				Random random=new Random();
				s=(int) (Math.random()*20+1);
				System.out.println(s);
				edit_text_area.setFont(new Font(\"宋体\",Font.PLAIN,s));
			}	
		});
		item_exit.addActionListener(new ActionListener(){
			public void actionPerformed(ActionEvent e) {
				System.exit(0);
			}	
		});
	}	
	public static void main(String[] args) {
		Demo4 demo4 = new Demo4();
	}
}')
